// mob_skill_db.txt, Monster Skill Database
//
// Structure of Database:
//
// MobID,Dummy(MobName@SkillName),State,SkillID,SkillLv,Rate,CastTime,Delay,Cancellable,Target,ConditionType,Val1,Val2,Val3,Val4,Val5,Emotion
//
// Example:
// 1001,Poring@TF_POISON,attack,52,3,100,1500,10000,no,target,always,0,,,,,7
//
// 'MobID': The ID of the monster that will be using the skill entry.
// 'Dummy(MobName@SkillName)': A parameter that's not actually loaded, used as a mob name/skill description for developers.
//
// 'State':
//	any			Any state (Except dead).
//	idle			In standby.
//	walk			In movement.
//	dead			Activated upon death.
//	loot			Picking up items (Like Poring).
//	attack			Attacking target.
//	chase			Chasing to attack target.
//
// 'SkillID': The ID of the skill that will be activated by the monster.
// 'SkillLv': The level of the skill that will be activated.
// 'Rate': The chance of the skill being casted when the condition is fulfilled (10000 = 100%).
// 'CastTime': The duration in milliseconds it takes for the skill to be casted.
// 'Delay': The duration in milliseconds that has to be pass before recasting the same skill.
// 'Cancellable': Whether or not the skill can be cancelled by being hit ('CastTime' must not be 0 for this to be valid).
//
// 'Target':
//	target			The monster's current target.
//	self			The monster itself.
//	friend			The monster's friend(s).
//	around			11x11 area around self.
//	around1			3x3 area around self.
//	around2			5x5 area around self.
//	around3			7x7 area around self.
//	around4			9x9 area around self.
//	around5			3x3 area around target.
//	around6			5x5 area around target.
//	around7			7x7 area around target.
//	around8			9x9 area around target.
//
// 'ConditionType':
//	always			Unconditional.
//	onspawn			When the mob spawns/respawns.
//	myhpltmaxrate		When the mob's hp drops to a certain percent.
//	friendhpltmaxrate	When the mob's friend's hp drops to a certain percent.
//	mystatuson		If the mob has any abnormalities in status (Condition value).
//	mystatusoff		If the mob has ended any abnormalities in status (Condition value).
//	friendstatuson		If the friend has any abnormalities in status (Condition value).
//	friendstatusoff		If the friend has ended any abnormalities in status (Condition value).
//	attackpcgt		Attack percentage becomes more than the  number of specification.
//	attackpcge		Attack percentage becomes equal or more than the number of specification.
//	slavelt			When the number of slaves is lower than the original number of specification.
//	slavele			When the number of slaves is lower or equal than the original number of specification.
//	closedattacked		When melee attacked (Close range attack).
//	longrangeattacked	When long ranged attacked (Like bows and far range weapons).
//	skillused		When a skill is used on the mob.
//	afterskill		After the mob uses certain skill.
//	casttargeted		When a target is in cast range.
//	rudeattacked		When a target is rude attacked.
//	masterattacked		When the monster's master is attacked.
//
// 'ConditionType' (Continued):
//	anybad			Any type of state change.
//	stone			Condition of being in stone state.
//	freeze			Condition of being in frozen state.
//	stun			Condition of being in stunned state.
//	sleep			Condition of being in sleep state.
//	poison			Condition of being in poisoned state.
//	curse			Condition of being in cursed state.
//	silence			Condition of being in silenced state.
//	confusion		Condition of being in confusion state.
//	blind			Condition of being in blind state.
//	hiding			Condition of being in hidden state.
//	sight			Condition of being in unhidden state.
//
// 'Val1/Val2/Val3/Val4/Val5': These are special parameters used depending on the used skill.
// 'Emotion': The ID of the emotion (aka emoticon) displayed by the client on the monster when the skill is used.
